### Post by iceman2048 on 2009-11-27
Bump,

Seems the problem is specifically with how K3B burns those dvd files. I tried using DvdShrink (via WINE) and converted the files to an iso. Then, I burned the iso with K3b and that worked flawlessly.

I stumbled across an app called k9copy that seems to serve the same purpose as dvdshrink. Will try that one next time.
